{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2022-03-14 16:15:09","updatedTime":"2022-03-14 16:15:09","title":"Alex Proba’s Collaboration With Gossamer Takes Rugs To a New High","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=474716","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/alex-probas-collaboration-with-gossamer-takes-rugs-to-a-new-high/alex-proba-gossamer-rugs-featured-1/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/alex-proba-gossamer-rugs-featured-1-810x555.jpg\" alt=\"Alex Proba&#8217;s Collaboration With Gossamer Takes Rugs To a New High\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Multidisciplinary artist <a href=\"https://www.studioproba.com/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><strong>Alex Proba</strong></a> – known for her distinct visual language that involves playful exploration of textures, shapes, and colors – has added another collection under her eponymous line <a href=\"https://probahome.com/textile-shop\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"><strong>Proba Home</strong></a>. In collaboration with <a href=\"https://www.gossamer.co/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><strong>Gossamer</strong></a>, a lifestyle cannabis brand, Alex has designed a colorful collection of four handwoven, hand-tufted rugs inspired by Gossamer’s color palette and the cover of its latest bi-annual magazine, <em>Volume Seven: Touch</em>.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/alex-probas-collaboration-with-gossamer-takes-rugs-to-a-new-high/alex-proba-gossamer-rugs-34/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-474753\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-474753\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/alex-proba-gossamer-rugs-34-810x1080.jpg\" alt=\"Alex Proba Gossamer rug collage\" width=\"810\" height=\"1080\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/alex-proba-gossamer-rugs-34-810x1080.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/alex-proba-gossamer-rugs-34-800x1066.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/alex-proba-gossamer-rugs-34-768x1024.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/alex-proba-gossamer-rugs-34-1152x1536.jpg 1152w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/alex-proba-gossamer-rugs-34.jpg 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The design process involved explorative collaging and multiple iterations once the collages were digitized. On giving proper nod to Gossamer, Alex shares, “We’ve added a smoky, psychedelic wave pattern as a subtle nod to Gossamer’s perspective and took cues from their typography, which is never just linear.” Alex’s signature shapes and patterns were then layered on top, a party of long white ribbons, drips of neon orange, polka dot cut-outs, and scallop swaths of baby pink.</p>\n<p><a The patterns are graphic and minimal: Vertigo is an abstract, geometric pattern, Tassel is an asymmetrical pattern with a relaxed expression, and Trapez features a tessellated design. Available in three shapes, its design was inspired by the ancient Japanese art of flowering arranging – that&#8217;s right, ikebana. The mouth-blown glass and metal vase will bring out the best in everything from roses to weeds.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475111\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-475111\" next level, courtesy of a curated collection of fabrics. Chosen by Jaime Hayon, the contemporary, colorful options were inspired by his travels to Thailand. Exclusive premium upholstery fabrics accentuate the chairs&#8217; frames and cushions, and are offered in shades ranging from subdued to statement making. Atom – designed by Raf Simons for Kvadrat – is a bold, wool-blend bouclé with a speckled appearance. Worsted wool Steelcut is a classic fabric in a new combination with tonal colors lending subtle, durable texture. The gently ribbed chenille Nabis accentuates the chairs with its parallel ribbed pattern and tactile finish.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475109\" rel=\"attachment Estates","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=475548","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Shut up and take ALL of my money! If ever there was a perfect mid-century inspired house outfitted with modern necessities, seamless California indoor/outdoor living, and panoramic views of the city and ocean, it would be this one by <a href=\"https://kovacdesignstudio.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"><strong>Kovac Design Studio</strong></a>. Situated towards the top of the famed Trousdale Estates in Beverly Hills, the <strong>Breeze Blocks</strong> residence is owned by an East Coast-based couple that loves to entertain friends when in town. Kovac Design Studio fulfilled their request of making the most of the stunning views and indoor/outdoor flow with a dream-worthy backyard.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475550\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-475550\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-475550\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/Breeze-Blocks-House-Kovac-Design-Studio-2-810x608.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"608\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/Breeze-Blocks-House-Kovac-Design-Studio-2-810x608.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/Breeze-Blocks-House-Kovac-Design-Studio-2-800x600.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/Breeze-Blocks-House-Kovac-Design-Studio-2-768x576.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/Breeze-Blocks-House-Kovac-Design-Studio-2.jpg 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The front of the home presents a series of breeze blocks, hence the project&#8217;s name, that form a privacy screen to prevent prying eyes from the street. The block walls also create a walkway to the front door where a lily pond and Burle-Max inspired glass mosaic wall panel greet visitors. A circular cutout in the roof brings natural light into the space with a bonus view of the sky.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475551\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-475551\" More","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=475668","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/f5-reetika-vijay-shares-her-culture-a-daily-wind-down-routine-more/f5-reetika-vijay-wayfair-boston-featured-image/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Wayfair-Boston-Featured-Image-810x540.png\" alt=\"F5: Reetika Vijay Shares Her Culture, a Daily Wind-Down Routine + More\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/reetika-vijay-aia-leed-ap-5391a321\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"><strong>Reetika Vijay</strong></a> is the Managing Principal for <a href=\"https://interiorarchitects.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"><strong>IA Interior Architects&#8217;</strong></a> Boston office. She brings with her over 25 years of experience in a leading role of strategic planning, managing, designing, administering, and negotiating a wide variety of project types. Reetika and her team are responsible for the design of millions of square feet of workplace, each impacting and improving lives.</p>\n<p>In addition to her role in Boston, Reetika serves on the IA Interior Architects Enterprise Leadership Team, and is also the founder and executive sponsor for IAReach, a firm-wide program supporting local and global charitable initiatives throughout IA’s global footprint. She holds several honors, such as Boston Real Estate Time’s 2019 Top 10 Most Influential Women, India New England’s Outstanding Women of 2020, and Interior Design Magazine’s HiP For Greater Good Award Winner in 2021. Reetika also serves on the Advisory Board for Massachusetts Center for Prevention of Cruelty Against Children. When not at work, she can be found spending her time in Wayland, Massachusetts with her husband and two children.</p>\n<p>Today, Reetika joins us for <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/column/friday-five/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><strong>Friday Five</strong></a>!</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475691\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-475691\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-475691\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Portrait-810x810.png\" alt=\"brown-skinned woman with long dark hair wearing a royal blue shirt and pearl necklace\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Portrait-810x810.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Portrait-800x800.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Portrait-100x100.png 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Portrait-768x768.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Portrait-300x300.png 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Portrait.png 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475697\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-475697\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-475697\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Yoga-810x560.png\" alt=\"two people doing seated while doing yoga\" width=\"810\" height=\"560\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Yoga-810x560.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Yoga-800x553.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Yoga-768x531.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Yoga.png 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<h2>1. YHS (Yoga, Hydrate, Shower)</h2>\n<p>The Jersey Shore gang had GTL (gym, tan, laundry), I have YHS (yoga, hydrate, shower). The stress of each day can take a toll as we juggle work, family, and life. YHS is what I selfishly consider my self-care time every evening. I usually begin with an escape to a curated environment: warmth, fireplace, dim lights, and aromatics. It&#8217;s amazing how powerful environment can be in the space of mind and body. The act of Yoga draws the stressors from my brain and muscles. Post-yoga hydration “cleanses” the toxins and a hot shower is the finishing touch, washing away all of the stress from my  day. The entire act of YHS is purifying for me, both emotionally and physically, enabling me to rise to conquer the following day.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475693\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-475693\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-475693\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Sparklers-810x558.png\" alt=\"four outstretched arms holding lit sparklers\" width=\"810\" height=\"558\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Sparklers-810x558.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Sparklers-800x551.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Sparklers-768x529.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Sparklers.png 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<h2>2. Sparkle</h2>\n<p>I love sparkle. It comes in many shapes and forms, but the obvious representation is physical: bling! I love it on my clothes, my accessories, and especially my design accents. The proper impact requires balance, and when personalized correctly provides that eye-catching lift in spirit, energy, and style. Sparkle comes in intangible forms, as well. It presents itself in people, in conversations, and in moments. This type of sparkle is not always obvious, but when drawn out brings dimensionality to what could be a very singular interaction. I look for sparkle in the staff I hire, the friendships I build, and the activities I pursue. All of these bring joy to my life.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475690\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-475690\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-475690\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Paisanos-810x578.png\" alt=\"collage of 12 images of people enjoying themselves in a restaurant\" width=\"810\" height=\"578\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Paisanos-810x578.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Paisanos-800x571.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Paisanos-768x548.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Paisanos.png 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<h2>3. Paisanos</h2>\n<p>For almost every Saturday night over the past 15 years, my husband, my children, and I have frequented the same Waltham, Massachusetts Mexican/Guatemalan restaurant. Some call us crazy, some call us loyal, but everyone questions what is driving our love for this one restaurant. Paisanos is not glamorous, it&#8217;s not fine dining, and you will never find it on any list of Michelin starred restaurants. It&#8217;s a hole-in-the wall with great food, local characters, and the best margaritas in town. Upon entry, you&#8217;re greeted by the colorful personalities of waitstaff and regulars. The wood-adorned Latin-themed interiors, TV screens alternating sports, and Keno provide a cozy yet active backdrop. Paisanos is more than a restaurant, it&#8217;s an evolving memory for my family and I.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475689\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-475689\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-475689\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Mountain-and-Water-Landscape-810x281.png\" alt=\"panoramic landscape of two mountains and a large bod off water against a cloudy blue sky\" width=\"810\" height=\"281\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Mountain-and-Water-Landscape-810x281.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Mountain-and-Water-Landscape-800x278.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Mountain-and-Water-Landscape-768x267.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Mountain-and-Water-Landscape.png 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<h2>4. Landscapes</h2>\n<p>I find landscapes extremely soothing. How can something so unplanned, so organic, so alive be equally as balanced, dimensional, and textured? They transform location to location, day to day, season to season. Desert, forest, mountains, ocean… all delight the senses with sound, smell, touch, and sight. No matter what culture, what political persuasion, what experiences one brings, we can all come together to admire natural beauty. Landscape inspires me when it comes to design. I strive to translate the inherent principles of nature into a built environment that enchants.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475688\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-475688\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-475688\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Indian-Textile-Pillows-810x540.png\" alt=\"three Indian textile pillows in shades of gold\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Indian-Textile-Pillows-810x540.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Indian-Textile-Pillows-800x534.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Indian-Textile-Pillows-768x512.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/03/F5-Reetika-Vijay-Indian-Textile-Pillows.png 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<h2>5. Indian Influences</h2>\n<p>When people find out I was born in India, they hardly believe me. Admittedly, we moved from New Delhi, India when I was only one, and my entire childhood was spent in Maine. I married an American (non-Indian) man and speak little Hindi. I am still Indian, however, and very proud of my heritage. Wherever I can, I showcase my culture. My home is adorned with Indian accents: artwork, pillows, jewel and gold tones. There is something so elegant in a neutral, modern palette accented by culture and tradition. I cook Indian meals and am beyond excited that they have become my children’s favorite. And Bollywood? I follow the biggest stars on Instagram, paying attention to fashion and happenings alike. I am Indian and very proud of it!</p>\n<h2><em>Work by Reetika Vijay:</em></h2>\n<div id=\"attachment_475687\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475687\" manufacturer <a href=\"https://www.scp.co.uk/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><strong>SCP</strong></a> is showcasing a collection by British designer <a href=\"https://maxlamb.org/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><strong>Max Lamb</strong></a> for ceramics brand <a href=\"https://1882ltd.com\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><strong>1882 Ltd.</strong></a> throughout the month of March. Titled <a href=\"https://www.scp.co.uk/collections/max-lamb-crockery-collection\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><strong>Crockery</strong></a>, the collection consists of fine bone china tablewares and vases that look crude and rock-like but are actually refined and lightweight.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475359\" rugs. The fact that her creative wonderland is a tiny little town in the Mojave Desert (specifically: Inyokern, “Sunshine Capital of America,” population 988).</p>\n<p><iframe loading=\"lazy\" title=\"YouTube video player\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/xeEFPhrtZ_w\" width=\"810\" height=\"455\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"><span data-mce-type=\"bookmark\" style=\"display: inline-block; width: 0px; overflow: hidden; line-height: 0;\" class=\"mce_SELRES_start\">?</span></iframe></p>\n<p>“I moved out here because I was able to take a lot of risks and have low overhead and plenty of space, with little distractions,” says Stern, who describes her family’s property here as a “salvage junk yard, [with] a bunch of rundown trailers and shipping containers.” They’re just part of the landscape in the gorgeous Mojave, about 80 miles south of Death Valley. “It&#8217;s so beautiful in the desert. It&#8217;s probably my favorite environment to be in. It was a great decision.”</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475506\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-475506\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone images of her work, including her snake-centric rugs, rainbow ceramics, and ghost figures. (From her bio: “Her goal as an artist is to make people feel happy when they see her work with subjects related to nature, celebration, and death.”) We asked Lorien about how her work reveals the influence of her father, a jeweler who was interested in alchemy. “He passed away, so that experience of his death is a big influence on my work,” she says. “And I guess his interest in alchemy has just made me think outside of the box. I know that he would approve of all the weird risks I&#8217;m taking.” Those risks might be at play when we ask her about her dream collaborations, following a gorgeous collection made with Seattle glass artist Austin Stern (no relation): “My dream collaboration would be a theme park or a cemetery,” she says. “So all you theme parks out there, talk to me! Send me an email.”</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=475508\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-475508\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large they are shown against a grass-green tufted background (where the snakes are lower than the “grass”) or a tan-colored “sand” background (where the snakes are higher.) If you love color, ghosts, imagination, the desert, rainbows – don’t miss this one! /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Hungary-born, Portland-based designer<a href=\"https://www.akoshuber.com/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><strong> Ákos Huber</strong></a> wanted to explore alternative ways of constructing a <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/furniture\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">chair</a> other than the typical symmetrical and perpendicular build. Taking inspiration from fishing structures that are cantilevered over the sea, he designed the <strong>Chair of the Moment</strong>, a seemingly random structure but was actually built with much purpose and intention.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=471894\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-471894\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-471894\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/01/akos-huber-chair-of-the-moment-4-810x1049.jpg\" alt=\"wooden chair\" width=\"810\" height=\"1049\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/01/akos-huber-chair-of-the-moment-4-810x1049.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/01/akos-huber-chair-of-the-moment-4-800x1036.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/01/akos-huber-chair-of-the-moment-4-768x994.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/01/akos-huber-chair-of-the-moment-4.jpg 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<blockquote class=\"instagram-media\" style=\"background: #FFF; margin-top: 8px; overflow: hidden; padding: 8px 0 7px; text-align: center; text-overflow: ellipsis; white-space: nowrap;\"><a style=\"color: #c9c8cd; font-family: Arial,sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: 17px; text-decoration: none;\" href=\"https://www.instagram.com/p/CW7f1nVrCsZ/?utm_source=ig_embed&#38;utm_campaign=loading\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">A post shared by Ákos Huber (@akoshuber)</a></p>\n</div>\n</blockquote>\n<p><script async src=\"//www.instagram.com/embed.js\"></script></p>\n<p>The Chair of the Moment has a modified pinwheel arrangement made up of seven angular white oak rods that are all connected with dowel joints to form a closed circuit. This in turn creates a reciprocal frame where each rod reclines on the previous one, making the entire structure stable. The backrest features an adjustable ball joint that allows the user to adjust their position. The seat is made of canvas to pair well with the white oak and create a comfortable seat.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=471902\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-471902\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-1-810x613.jpg\" alt=\"Side profile of rose bronze and black aluminum scooter parked against wall with window backdrop and ground with circular concrete.\" width=\"810\" height=\"613\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-1-810x613.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-1-800x605.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-1-768x581.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-1.jpg 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Alongside evoking the Bauhaus&#8217; &#8220;form follows function,&#8221; NAON also cites Dieter Rams&#8217; <a href=\"https://designmuseum.org/discover-design/all-stories/what-is-good-design-a-quick-look-at-dieter-rams-ten-principles\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">10 commandments for good design</a> as the guiding principles that help shape their Zero-One&#8217;s sleek minimalist approach to mobility.</p>\n<blockquote><p><strong><em>&#8220;&#8230;our aluminium parts are anodised to protect against corrosion and the transparent windscreen is treated with a multi-resist coating to protect against abrasion and UV radiation. Not only does this increase the lifespan of individual components, but it ensures that they continue to operate at their maximum efficiency.&#8221;</em></strong></p></blockquote>\n<div id=\"attachment_474834\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=474834\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-474834\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-474834 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-3-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"Detail of scooter's floorboard foot platform where batteries are stored underneath, imprinted with NAON logo.\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-3-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-3-800x534.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-3-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-3.jpg 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">The scooter can store up to two removable battery packs under the floorboards, each 2.4kWh battery offering 70km of range and up to 140km when both are fully charged. Each battery can be charged in place or removed using a supplied charging unit.</p></div>\n<p>The Zero-One is primarily comprised of the aforementioned aluminum, alongside recycled PET plastic for non-structural components of the scooter. Aluminum sections are laser cut and pressed to construct the main frame of the scooter to minimize waste. Additionally NAON mirrors the trend within the automotive industry toward using recycled and ecological materials across parts where rider and machine often touch; for example the handlebar and footrest grips contain recycled shredded rubber, and the organic faux leather seat trim is manufactured from cactus skin.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=474835\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-474835\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-474835\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-4-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-4-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-4-800x534.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-4-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-4.jpg 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The Zero-One will come in two flavors, the first L1e offering a more sedate top speed of 28mph, and the L3e&#8217;s larger 13hp engine capable of a top speed over 62mph.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=474836\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-474836\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-474836\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-21-copy-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-21-copy.jpg 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_474833\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=474833\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-474833\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-474833 size-large\" https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-2-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2022/02/NAON_MOBILITY_Aleksander_Ziarnecki-2.jpg 1180w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">The Zero-One&#8217;s suspension combined with a low center of gravity produced by the battery storage across the floorboard offers a stable and balanced ride at any speed or across most urban road surfaces.</p></div>\n<p>NAON&#8217;s designers also factored in aspects of end of life considerations when speccing their two-wheel vehicle, making the Zero-One not only easy to refurbish, upgrade, or replace any components over its lifespan, but also manufactured with materials that can easily be separated and recycled when the scooter has reached its final mile.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=474837\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-474837\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\"
